TITLE       Double, single differential neutron emission and      2210600100003 
            total cross sections at 14.1 MeV for B-10, B-11       2210600100004 
            and Bi-209                                            2210600100005 
AUTHOR     (A.Takahashi, M.Gotoh, Y.Sasaki, H.Sugimoto)           2210600100006 
INSTITUTE  (2JPNOSA)                                              2210600100007 
REFERENCE  (R,OKTAV-A-92-01,1992)                                 2210600100008 
            Tables (ADX,SIG,EDX,DDX) and figs (ADX,EDX,DDX) given 2210600100009 
           (S,JAERI-M-88-102,1988)                                2210600100010 
            Slightly different tabulated ADX and SIG given        2210600100011 
REL-REF    (M,,E.Ishimura+,R,OKTAV-A-87-02,1987)                  2210600100012 
            Correction calculations and MUSCC3 code description   2210600100013 
           (M,,A.Takahashi,J,NST,25,215,1988)                     2210600100014 
            Experimental method in detail                         2210600100015 
FACILITY   (CCW,2JPNOSA) OKTAVIAN facility at Osaka University.   2210600100016 
            Operated with a pulsed deuteron beam of 2 ns pulse    2210600100017 
            width and 1 MHz repetition rate.                      2210600100018 
INC-SOURCE (D-T) 14 MeV neutrons generated at a Ti-T target       2210600100019 
METHOD     (TOF) Time-of-flight with flight path of 8.3 m fixed   2210600100020 
            in the 85 degrees direction. The scattering angles    2210600100021 
            were changed by moving the sample on an arch, located 2210600100022 
            17 cm radially apart from the t-target.               2210600100023 
DETECTOR   (SCIN) A 25.4 cm diameter by 10 cm thick NE-213 liquid 2210600100024 
            scintillator was used to measure the angular distri-  2210600100025 
            butions of scattered neutrons. The detector had       2210600100026 
            excellent n-gamma discrimination for a dynamic range  2210600100027 
            of 0.5 to 14 MeV in recoil proton energy. A specially 2210600100028 
            shaped shadow bar and collimator shield eliminated    2210600100029 
            the background efficiently.                           2210600100030 
MONITOR    (1-H-1(N,EL)1-H-1,,DA)                                 2210600100031 
CORRECTION  Corrections are made for                              2210600100032 
             - multiple scattering;                               2210600100033 
             - attenuation;                                       2210600100034 
             - neutron source contamination.                      2210600100035 
            based on JENDL-3. In case that JENDL-3 would produce  2210600100036 
            double differential neutron emission spectrum in      2210600100037 
            drastic disagreement with the measured one, the       2210600100038 
            correction can be failed and the adoption of RAW data 2210600100039 
            is recommended by authors.                            2210600100040 
COMMENT    .Correction factor are calculated using evaluated data,2210600100041 
            however, they are still primitive. Calculation of cor-2210600100042 
            rection factors should be carried out again after new 2210600100043 
            version of evaluation would be published.             2210600100044 
SAMPLE     .The B-10, B-11 and Bi-209 samples were a cylinders    2210600100045 
            of 3 cm diameter and 7.0 cm length.                   2210600100046 
           .The monitor sample was a cylinder of polyethylene with2210600100047 
            1.5 cm diameter by 5 cm in height.                    2210600100048 
            Samples placed at 17 cm point                         2210600100049 
           .Background runs were performed with an empty aluminum 2210600100050 
            can (B-10, B-11) and with no sample at all.           2210600100051
